//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/President_Puigdemont%2C_%22Ciutadans_de_Catalunya%2C_v%C3%A9nen_hores_en_qu%C3%A8_a_tots_ens_pertocar%C3%A0_de_mantenir_el_pols_del_nostre_pa%C3%ADs%22_02.jpg/440px-President_Puigdemont%2C_%22Ciutadans_de_Catalunya%2C_v%C3%A9nen_hores_en_qu%C3%A8_a_tots_ens_pertocar%C3%A0_de_mantenir_el_pols_del_nostre_pa%C3%ADs%22_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3840" data-file-height="2560" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:President_Puigdemont,_%22Ciutadans_de_Catalunya,_v%C3%A9nen_hores_en_qu%C3%A8_a_tots_ens_pertocar%C3%A0_de_mantenir_el_pols_del_nostre_pa%C3%ADs%22_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Generalitat_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="President of the Generalitat of Catalonia">Catalan president</a>, <a href="/wiki/Carles_Puigdemont" title="Carles Puigdemont">Carles Puigdemont</a>, addresses to the crowd following the unilateral declaration of independence on 27 October</div></div></div>
<p>A controversial <a href="/wiki/2017_Catalan_independence_referendum" title="2017 Catalan independence referendum">independence referendum</a> was held in Catalonia on 1 October 2017, using a disputed voting process.<sup id="cite_ref-ElPais03102017_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ElPais03102017-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> It was declared illegal and suspended by the <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Spain" title="Constitutional Court of Spain">Constitutional Court of Spain</a>, because it breached the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Constitution_of_1978" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Constitution of 1978">1978 Constitution</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-boe2162017_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-boe2162017-56">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Subsequent developments saw, on 27 October 2017, a symbolic <a href="/wiki/Catalan_declaration_of_independence" title="Catalan declaration of independence">declaration of independence</a> by the Parliament of Catalonia, the enforcement of <a href="/wiki/Direct_rule_over_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct rule over Catalonia">direct rule</a> by the Spanish government through the use of Article 155 of the Constitution,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> the dismissal of the <a href="/wiki/Executive_Council_of_Catalonia" title="Executive Council of Catalonia">Executive Council</a> and the dissolution of the Parliament, with a <a href="/wiki/2017_Catalan_regional_election" title="2017 Catalan regional election">snap regional election</a> called for 21 December 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-eldiario.es-27Oct17_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eldiario.es-27Oct17-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Former President <a href="/wiki/Carles_Puigdemont" title="Carles Puigdemont">Carles Puigdemont</a> and five former cabinet ministers fled Spain, whereas nine other cabinet members, including vice-president <a href="/wiki/Oriol_Junqueras" title="Oriol Junqueras">Oriol Junqueras</a>, were jailed under various charges of rebellion, sedition, and misuse of public funds.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Quim_Torra" title="Quim Torra">Quim Torra</a> became the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_the_Government_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of the Government of Catalonia">131st</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Government_of_Catalonia" title="President of the Government of Catalonia">President of the Government of Catalonia</a> on 17 May 2018,<sup id="cite_ref-GeneralitatdeCataluny17052018_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GeneralitatdeCataluny17052018-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> after the Spanish courts blocked three other candidates.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2018, the <a href="/wiki/Assemblea_Nacional_Catalana" title="Assemblea Nacional Catalana">Assemblea Nacional Catalana</a> joined the <a href="/wiki/Unrepresented_Nations_and_Peoples_Organization" title="Unrepresented Nations and Peoples Organization">Unrepresented Nations and Peoples Organization</a> (UNPO) on behalf of Catalonia.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">Geography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Geography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">Climate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Climate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png/220px-Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="207" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png/330px-Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png/440px-Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png 2x" data-file-width="3128" data-file-height="2944" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mapa_clim%C3%A0tic_de_Catalunya.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Climates of Catalonia: <div class="plainlist"><ul><li><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #00A86B; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Oceanic_climate" title="Oceanic climate">Oceanic climate</a></div></li><li><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #9966CC; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Alpine_climate" title="Alpine climate">Alpine climate</a></div></li><li><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #77B5FE; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Mediterranean climate of alpine influence</div></li><li><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FFE5B4; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Inland Mediterranean climate</div></li><li><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FF7F00; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_climate" title="Mediterranean climate">Coastal Mediterranean climate</a></div></li><li><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FF9271; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Mediterranean climate of <a href="/wiki/Continental_climate" title="Continental climate">continental influence</a></div></li></ul></div></div></div></div>
<p>The climate of Catalonia is diverse. The populated areas lying by the coast in Tarragona, Barcelona and Girona provinces feature a <a href="/wiki/Hot-summer_Mediterranean_climate" class="mw-redirect" title="Hot-summer Mediterranean climate">Hot-summer Mediterranean climate</a> (<a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">Köppen</a> <i>Csa</i>). The inland part (including the Lleida province and the inner part of Barcelona province) show a mostly <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_climate" title="Mediterranean climate">Mediterranean climate</a> (<a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">Köppen</a> <i>Csa</i>). The Pyrenean peaks have a <a href="/wiki/Continental_climate" title="Continental climate">continental</a> (<a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">Köppen</a> <i>D</i>) or even <a href="/wiki/Alpine_climate" title="Alpine climate">Alpine climate</a> (<a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">Köppen</a> <i>ET</i>) at the highest summits, while the valleys have a maritime or <a href="/wiki/Oceanic_climate" title="Oceanic climate">oceanic climate</a> sub-type (<a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="Köppen climate classification">Köppen</a> <i>Cfb</i>).
</p><p>In the Mediterranean area, summers are dry and hot with sea breezes, and the maximum temperature is around 26–31&#160;°C (79–88&#160;°F). Winter is cool or slightly cold depending on the location. It snows frequently in the Pyrenees, and it occasionally snows at lower altitudes, even by the coastline. Spring and autumn are typically the rainiest seasons, except for the Pyrenean valleys, where summer is typically stormy.
</p><p>The inland part of Catalonia is hotter and drier in summer. Temperature may reach 35&#160;°C (95&#160;°F), some days even 40&#160;°C (104&#160;°F). Nights are cooler there than at the coast, with the temperature of around 14–17&#160;°C (57–63&#160;°F). Fog is not uncommon in valleys and plains; it can be especially persistent, with <a href="/wiki/Freezing_drizzle" title="Freezing drizzle">freezing drizzle</a> episodes and subzero temperatures during winter, mainly along the <a href="/wiki/Ebro" title="Ebro">Ebro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Segre_River" class="mw-redirect" title="Segre River">Segre</a> valleys and in <a href="/wiki/Plain_of_Vic" title="Plain of Vic">Plain of Vic</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Topography">Topography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Topography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_mountains_in_Catalonia" title="List of mountains in Catalonia">List of mountains in Catalonia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Catmorfo.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Catmorfo.png/220px-Catmorfo.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="213" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Catmorfo.png/330px-Catmorfo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Catmorfo.png/440px-Catmorfo.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="968" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Catmorfo.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Geomorphologic" class="mw-redirect" title="Geomorphologic">Geomorphologic</a> map of Catalonia: <div class="plainlist"><ul><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#ff3f3f; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pyrenees" title="Pyrenees">Pyrenees</a> </span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#ffa545; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Pre-Pyrenees" title="Pre-Pyrenees">Pre-Pyrenees</a> </span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#fff915; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catalan_Central_Depression" title="Catalan Central Depression">Catalan Central Depression</a></span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#d8c03d; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Smaller mountain ranges of the Central Depression </span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#917654; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catalan_Transversal_Range" title="Catalan Transversal Range">Catalan Transversal Range</a> </span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#487048; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catalan_Pre-Coastal_Range" title="Catalan Pre-Coastal Range">Catalan Pre-Coastal Range</a> </span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#679772; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catalan_Coastal_Range" title="Catalan Coastal Range">Catalan Coastal Range</a> </span></li><li><span style="margin:0; font-size:90%; white-space:nowrap;"><span class="legend-text" style="border:none; padding:1px .6em; background-color:#a0d486; color:black; font-size:95%; line-height:1.25; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catalan_Coastal_Depression" title="Catalan Coastal Depression">Catalan Coastal Depression</a> and other coastal and pre-coastal plains</span></li></ul></div></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beciberri.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Beciberri.JPG/220px-Beciberri.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Beciberri.JPG/330px-Beciberri.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Beciberri.JPG/440px-Beciberri.JPG 2x" data-file-width="2272" data-file-height="1704" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beciberri.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Besiberri" class="mw-redirect" title="Besiberri">Besiberri</a> in Catalan <a href="/wiki/Pyrenees" title="Pyrenees">Pyrenees</a></div></div></div>
<p>Catalonia has a marked geographical diversity, considering the relatively small size of its territory. The <a href="/wiki/Geography" title="Geography">geography</a> is conditioned by the Mediterranean coast, with 580 kilometres (360 miles) of coastline, and large relief units of the Pyrenees to the north. The Catalan territory is divided into three main geomorphological units:<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>The Pyrenees: mountainous formation that connects the Iberian Peninsula with the <a href="/wiki/Continental_Europe" title="Continental Europe">European continental territory</a>, and located in the north of Catalonia;</li>
<li>The Catalan Coastal mountain ranges or the Catalan Mediterranean System: an alternating delevacions and planes parallel to the Mediterranean coast;</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Catalan_Central_Depression" title="Catalan Central Depression">Catalan Central Depression</a>: structural unit which forms the eastern sector of the Valley of the Ebro.</li></ul>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2012_Montserrat.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/2012_Montserrat.jpg/220px-2012_Montserrat.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/2012_Montserrat.jpg/330px-2012_Montserrat.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ae/2012_Montserrat.jpg/440px-2012_Montserrat.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3888" data-file-height="2592" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2012_Montserrat.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mountain of <a href="/wiki/Montserrat_(mountain)" title="Montserrat (mountain)">Montserrat</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Santa_Maria_de_Montserrat_Abbey" title="Santa Maria de Montserrat Abbey">monastery</a></div></div></div>
<p>The Catalan Pyrenees represent almost half in length of the Pyrenees, as it extends more than 200 kilometres (120 miles). Traditionally differentiated the Axial Pyrenees (the main part) and the <a href="/wiki/Pre-Pyrenees" title="Pre-Pyrenees">Pre-Pyrenees</a> (southern from the Axial) which are mountainous formations parallel to the main mountain ranges but with lower altitudes, less steep and a different geological formation. The highest mountain of Catalonia, located north of the comarca of Pallars Sobirà is the Pica d'Estats (3,143&#160;m), followed by the Puigpedrós (2,914&#160;m). On the Pre-Pyrenees is located the <a href="/wiki/Serra_del_Cad%C3%AD" title="Serra del Cadí">Serra del Cadí</a>, that separates the valley of <a href="/wiki/Cerdanya" title="Cerdanya">Cerdanya</a> from the Central Depression.
</p><p>Central Catalan Depression is a plain located between the Pyrenees and Pre-Coastal Mountains. The Depression lands are located between 200 and 600 metres (660 and 1,970 feet). The plains and the water that descend from the Pyrenees have made it fertile territory for <a href="/wiki/Agriculture" title="Agriculture">agriculture</a> and there are built numerous irrigation canals. Other important plain is the <a href="/wiki/Empord%C3%A0" title="Empordà">Empordà</a>, located on the northeast.
</p><p>The Catalan Mediterranean system is based on two (more or less) parallel ranges to the coast, in a Northwest direction towards the Southwest. These two mountain ranges are the Coastal and the Pre-Coastal. The Coastal Range is minor extent and it has lower altitudes, while the Pre-Coastal is larger in both length and height. The most relevant mountains of this area are <a href="/wiki/Montserrat_(mountain)" title="Montserrat (mountain)">Montserrat</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montseny_Massif" title="Montseny Massif">Montseny</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ports_de_Tortosa-Beseit" title="Ports de Tortosa-Beseit">Ports</a>. Within the ranges are a series of plains, the entities over which form the Coastal and the Pre-Coastal Depressions. The Coastal Depression is located on the East of the Coastal Range towards the coast. The Pre-Coastal, on the other hand, is located in the interior, between the two mountain ranges, and constitutes the basis of the plains of <a href="/wiki/Vall%C3%A8s" title="Vallès">Vallès</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pened%C3%A8s" title="Penedès">Penedès</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Flora_and_fauna">Flora and fauna</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Flora and fauna">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg/220px-BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg/330px-BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg/440px-BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4288" data-file-height="2848" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:BennyTrapp_Montseny-Gebirgsmolch_Calotriton_arnoldi_Montseny-Gebirge_Spanien.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Montseny brook newt (<i><a href="/wiki/Calotriton_arnoldi" class="mw-redirect" title="Calotriton arnoldi">Calotriton arnoldi</a></i>), <a href="/wiki/Endemic" class="mw-redirect" title="Endemic">endemic</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Montseny_Massif" title="Montseny Massif">Montseny Massif</a></div></div></div>
<p>Catalonia is a showcase of European <a href="/wiki/Landscapes" class="mw-redirect" title="Landscapes">landscapes</a> on a small scale. Just over 30,000 square kilometres (12,000 square miles) hosting a variety of substrates, soils, climates, directions, altitudes and distances to the sea. The area is of great ecological diversity and a remarkable wealth of landscapes, habitats and species.
</p><p>The fauna of Catalonia comprises a minority of animals endemic to the region and a majority of non-native animals. Much of Catalonia enjoys a Mediterranean climate (except mountain areas), which makes many of the animals that live there adapted to Mediterranean ecosystems. Of mammals, there are plentiful <a href="/wiki/Wild_boar" title="Wild boar">wild boar</a>, red foxes, as well as <a href="/wiki/Roe_deer" title="Roe deer">roe deer</a> and in the Pyrenees, the <a href="/wiki/Pyrenean_chamois" title="Pyrenean chamois">Pyrenean chamois</a>. Other large species such as the <a href="/wiki/Bear" title="Bear">bear</a> have been recently reintroduced.
</p><p>Waters of <a href="/wiki/Balearic_Sea" title="Balearic Sea">Balearic Sea</a> are rich in biodiversity, and even the <a href="/wiki/Megafauna" title="Megafauna">megafaunas</a> of ocean; various type of whales (such as <a href="/wiki/Fin_whale" title="Fin whale">fin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sperm_whale" title="Sperm whale">sperm</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Long-finned_pilot_whale" title="Long-finned pilot whale">pilot</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Dolphin" title="Dolphin">dolphins</a> live within the area.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hydrography">Hydrography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Hydrography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_rivers_of_Catalonia" title="List of rivers of Catalonia">List of rivers of Catalonia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png/220px-Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png/330px-Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png/440px-Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png 2x" data-file-width="2362" data-file-height="1523" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Aerea_estany_de_banyoles.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Lake_of_Banyoles" title="Lake of Banyoles">Lake of Banyoles</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG/220px-Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG/330px-Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2e/Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG/440px-Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3648" data-file-height="2736" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Tossa_de_Mar_Buchten_1.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Tossa_de_Mar" title="Tossa de Mar">Tossa de Mar</a>, Costa Brava</div></div></div>
<p>Most of Catalonia belongs to the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Basin" title="Mediterranean Basin">Mediterranean Basin</a>. The Catalan hydrographic network consists of two important basins, the one of the <a href="/wiki/Ebro" title="Ebro">Ebro</a> and the one that comprises the internal basins of Catalonia (respectively covering 46.84% and 51.43% of the territory), all of them flow to the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean" class="mw-redirect" title="Mediterranean">Mediterranean</a>. Furthermore, there is the <a href="/wiki/Garona" class="mw-redirect" title="Garona">Garona</a> river basin that flows to the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic Ocean</a>, but it only covers 1.73% of the Catalan territory.
</p><p>The hydrographic network can be divided in two sectors, an occidental slope or Ebro river slope and one oriental slope constituted by minor rivers that flow to the Mediterranean along the Catalan coast. The first slope provides an average of 18,700 <a href="/wiki/Cubic_metre" title="Cubic metre">cubic hectometres</a> (4.5 <a href="/wiki/Cubic_mile" title="Cubic mile">cubic miles</a>) per year, while the second only provides an average of 2,020&#160;hm<sup>3</sup> (0.48&#160;cu&#160;mi)/year. The difference is due to the big contribution of the Ebro river, from which the <a href="/wiki/Segre_(river)" title="Segre (river)">Segre</a> is an important tributary. Moreover, in Catalonia there is a relative wealth of groundwaters, although there is inequality between <i><a href="/wiki/Comarca" title="Comarca">comarques</a></i>, given the complex geological structure of the territory.<sup id="cite_ref-GEC_clima_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GEC_clima-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> In the Pyrenees there are many small lakes, remnants of the <a href="/wiki/Quaternary_glaciation" title="Quaternary glaciation">ice age</a>. The biggest are the <a href="/wiki/Lake_of_Banyoles" title="Lake of Banyoles">lake of Banyoles</a> and the recently recovered <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lake_of_Ivars&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Lake of Ivars (page does not exist)">lake of Ivars</a>.
</p><p>The Catalan coast is almost rectilinear, with a length of 580 kilometres (360&#160;mi) and few <a href="/wiki/Landform" title="Landform">landforms</a>—the most relevant are the <a href="/wiki/Cap_de_Creus" title="Cap de Creus">Cap de Creus</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Roses" title="Gulf of Roses">Gulf of Roses</a> to the north and the <a href="/wiki/Ebro_Delta" title="Ebro Delta">Ebro Delta</a> to the south. The <a href="/wiki/Catalan_Coastal_Range" title="Catalan Coastal Range">Catalan Coastal Range</a> hugs the coastline, and it is split into two segments, one between <a href="/wiki/L%27Estartit" title="L&#39;Estartit">L'Estartit</a> and the town of <a href="/wiki/Blanes" title="Blanes">Blanes</a> (the <a href="/wiki/Costa_Brava" title="Costa Brava">Costa Brava</a>), and the other at the south, at the Costes del <a href="/wiki/Garraf" title="Garraf">Garraf</a>.
</p><p>The principal <a href="/wiki/List_of_rivers_of_Catalonia" title="List of rivers of Catalonia">rivers in Catalonia</a> are the <a href="/wiki/Ter_(river)" title="Ter (river)">Ter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Llobregat" title="Llobregat">Llobregat</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Ebro" title="Ebro">Ebro</a> (Catalan: <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Ebre</i>), all of which run into the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean" class="mw-redirect" title="Mediterranean">Mediterranean</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Anthropic_pressure_and_protection_of_nature">Anthropic pressure and protection of nature</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Anthropic pressure and protection of nature">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The majority of Catalan population is concentrated in 30% of the territory, mainly in the coastal plains. Intensive agriculture, livestock farming and industrial activities have been accompanied by a massive <a href="/wiki/Mass_tourism" class="mw-redirect" title="Mass tourism">tourist</a> influx (more than 20 million annual visitors), a rate of urbanization and even of major metropolisation which has led to a strong urban sprawl: a third of Catalans live in the urban area of Barcelona, while the proportion of urbanized soils increased from 4.2% in 1993 to 6.2% in 2009, a growth of 48.6% in sixteen years, complemented with a dense network of transport infrastructure. This is accompanied by a certain agricultural abandonment (decrease of 15% of all areas cultivated in Catalonia between 1993 and 2009) and a global threat to <a href="/wiki/Natural_environment" title="Natural environment">natural environment</a>. Human activities have also put some animal species at risk, or even led to their disappearance from the territory, like the <a href="/wiki/Gray_wolf" class="mw-redirect" title="Gray wolf">gray wolf</a> and probably the <a href="/wiki/Brown_bear" title="Brown bear">brown bear</a> of the Pyrenees. The pressure created by this model of life means that the country's <a href="/wiki/Ecological_footprint" title="Ecological footprint">ecological footprint</a> exceeds its administrative area.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Faced with this problems, Catalan authorities initiated several measures whose purpose is to protect natural ecosystems. Thus, in 1990, the Catalan government created the Nature Conservation Council (Catalan: <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Consell de Protecció de la Natura</i>), an advisory body with the aim to study, protect and manage the natural environments and landscapes of Catalonia. In addition, the Generalitat has carried out the Plan of Spaces of Natural Interest (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Pla d'Espais d'Interès Natural</i> or PEIN) in 1992 while eighteen Natural Spaces of Special Protection (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Espais Naturals de Protecció Especial</i> or ENPE) have been instituted.
</p><p>There's a <a href="/wiki/National_Park" class="mw-redirect" title="National Park">National Park</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aig%C3%BCestortes_i_Estany_de_Sant_Maurici_National_Park" title="Aigüestortes i Estany de Sant Maurici National Park">Aigüestortes i Estany de Sant Maurici</a>; fourteen <a href="/wiki/Natural_park_(Spain)" title="Natural park (Spain)">Natural Parks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alt_Pirineu_Natural_Park" title="Alt Pirineu Natural Park">Alt Pirineu</a>, Aiguamolls de l'Empordà, <a href="/wiki/Cad%C3%AD-Moixer%C3%B3_Natural_Park" title="Cadí-Moixeró Natural Park">Cadí-Moixeró</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cap_de_Creus" title="Cap de Creus">Cap de Creus</a>, Sources of Ter and Freser, <a href="/wiki/Collserola" class="mw-redirect" title="Collserola">Collserola</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ebro_Delta" title="Ebro Delta">Ebro Delta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ports_de_Tortosa-Beseit" title="Ports de Tortosa-Beseit">Ports</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montgr%C3%AD,_Medes_Islands_and_Baix_Ter_Natural_Park" title="Montgrí, Medes Islands and Baix Ter Natural Park">Montgrí, Medes Islands and Baix Ter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montseny_Massif" title="Montseny Massif">Montseny</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montserrat" title="Montserrat">Montserrat</a>, Sant Llorenç del Munt and l'Obac, <a href="/wiki/Serra_de_Montsant" title="Serra de Montsant">Serra de Montsant</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Garrotxa_Volcanic_Zone_Natural_Park" title="Garrotxa Volcanic Zone Natural Park">Garrotxa Volcanic Zone</a>; as well as three Natural Places of National Interest (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Paratge Natural d'Interes Nacional</i> or PNIN), the <a href="/wiki/Pedraforca" title="Pedraforca">Pedraforca</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Poblet_Monastery" title="Poblet Monastery">Poblet</a> Forest and the <a href="/wiki/Alb%C3%A8res" class="mw-redirect" title="Albères">Albères</a>.
</p>

</div></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:right;font-size:115%;padding-top: 0.6em;"><div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Politics_of_Catalonia" title="Template:Politics of Catalonia"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Politics_of_Catalonia" title="Template talk:Politics of Catalonia"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Politics_of_Catalonia&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Catalonia" title="Politics of Catalonia">Politics of Catalonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Spain" title="Politics of Spain">Politics of Spain</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Catalan_independence" class="mw-redirect" title="Catalan independence">Catalan independence</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:142px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Lluis_Companys.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Lluis_Companys.jpg/140px-Lluis_Companys.jpg" decoding="async" width="140" height="225" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Lluis_Companys.jpg/210px-Lluis_Companys.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Lluis_Companys.jpg/280px-Lluis_Companys.jpg 2x" data-file-width="504" data-file-height="810" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Lluis_Companys.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Llu%C3%ADs_Companys" title="Lluís Companys">Lluís Companys</a>, second president of the Generalitat of Catalonia between 1933 and 1940, executed by Franco's regime</div></div></div>
<p>After Franco's death in 1975 and the adoption of a democratic constitution in Spain in 1978, Catalonia recovered and extended the powers that it had gained in the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Autonomy" title="Statute of Autonomy">Statute of Autonomy</a> of 1932<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> but lost with the fall of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Spanish_Republic" title="Second Spanish Republic">Second Spanish Republic</a><sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> at the end of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Civil_War" title="Spanish Civil War">Spanish Civil War</a> in 1939.
</p><p>This autonomous community has gradually achieved more <a href="/wiki/Self-governance" title="Self-governance">autonomy</a> since the approval of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Constitution_of_1978" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Constitution of 1978">Spanish Constitution of 1978</a>. The Generalitat holds exclusive jurisdiction in education, health, culture, environment, communications, transportation, commerce, public safety and local government, and only shares jurisdiction with the Spanish government in justice.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> In all, some analysts argue that formally the current system grants Catalonia with "more self-government than almost any other corner in Europe".<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The support for Catalan nationalism ranges from a demand for further autonomy and the <a href="/wiki/Federalisation" class="mw-redirect" title="Federalisation">federalisation</a> of Spain to the desire for independence from the rest of Spain, expressed by Catalan independentists.<sup id="cite_ref-CEO_poll_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CEO_poll-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> The first survey following the Constitutional Court ruling that cut back elements of the 2006 Statute of Autonomy, published by <i><a href="/wiki/La_Vanguardia" title="La Vanguardia">La Vanguardia</a></i> on 18 July 2010, found that 46% of the voters would support independence in a referendum.<sup id="cite_ref-La_Vanguardia_poll_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-La_Vanguardia_poll-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> In February of the same year, a poll by the <a href="/wiki/Open_University_of_Catalonia" title="Open University of Catalonia">Open University of Catalonia</a> gave more or less the same results.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Other polls have shown lower support for independence, ranging from 40 to 49%.<sup id="cite_ref-Cadenaser.com_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cadenaser.com-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-auto_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Lavanguardia.es_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lavanguardia.es-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> Although it is established in the whole of the territory, support for independence is significantly higher in the hinterland and the northeast, away from the more populated coastal areas such as Barcelona.<sup id="cite_ref-eldiario.es_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-eldiario.es-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Since 2011 when the question started to be regularly surveyed by the governmental Center for Public Opinion Studies (CEO), support for Catalan independence has been on the rise.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> According to the CEO opinion poll from July 2016, 47.7% of Catalans would vote for independence and 42.4% against it while, about the question of preferences, according to the CEO opinion poll from March 2016, a 57.2 claim to be "absolutely" or "fairly" in favour of independence.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Other polls have shown lower support for independence, ranging from 40 to 49%.<sup id="cite_ref-Cadenaser.com_81-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Cadenaser.com-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-auto_82-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Lavanguardia.es_83-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Lavanguardia.es-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> Other polls show more variable results, according with the Spanish CIS, as of December 2016, 47% of Catalans rejected independence and 45% supported it.<sup id="cite_ref-antena3.com_88-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-antena3.com-88">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In hundreds of non-binding local referendums on independence, organised across Catalonia from 13 September 2009, a large majority voted for independence, although critics argued that the polls were mostly held in pro-independence areas. In December 2009, 94% of those voting backed independence from Spain, on a turn-out of 25%.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> The final local referendum was held in Barcelona, in April 2011. On 11 September 2012, a pro-independence march pulled in a crowd of between 600,000 (according to the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Government" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Government">Spanish Government</a>), 1.5 million (according to the <a href="/wiki/Gu%C3%A0rdia_Urbana_de_Barcelona" title="Guàrdia Urbana de Barcelona">Guàrdia Urbana de Barcelona</a>), and 2 million (according to its promoters);<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> whereas poll results revealed that half the population of Catalonia supported secession from Spain.
</p>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r923042769/mw-parser-output/.tmulti"/><div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:442px;max-width:442px"><div class="trow"><div class="theader" style="text-align:center;background-color:transparent">Prominent Catalan politicians in <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a>.</div></div><div class="trow"><div class="tsingle" style="width:152px;max-width:152px"><div class="thumbimage"><a href="/wiki/File:Prim_madrazo.jpeg" class="image"><img alt="" href="/wiki/Juan_Prim,_1st_Marquis_of_los_Castillejos" class="mw-redirect" title="Juan Prim, 1st Marquis of los Castillejos">Juan Prim</a> (<a href="/wiki/Prime_minister_of_Spain" class="mw-redirect" title="Prime minister of Spain">Spanish prime minister</a> under regent <a href="/wiki/Francisco_Serrano,_1st_Duke_of_la_Torre" title="Francisco Serrano, 1st Duke of la Torre">don Francisco Serrano</a>)</div></div><div class="tsingle" style="width:123px;max-width:123px"><div class="thumbimage"><a href="/wiki/File:Figueras_y_Moragas.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Figueras_y_Moragas.jpg/121px-Figueras_y_Moragas.jpg" decoding="async" width="121" height="205" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/df/Figueras_y_Moragas.jpg/182px-Figueras_y_Moragas.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/df/Figueras_y_Moragas.jpg 2x" data-file-width="207" data-file-height="350" /></a></div><div class="thumbcaption"><a href="/wiki/Estanislao_Figueras" title="Estanislao Figueras">Estanislao Figueras</a> (president of the <a href="/wiki/First_Spanish_Republic" title="First Spanish Republic">First Spanish Republic</a>)</div></div><div class="tsingle" style="width:161px;max-width:161px"><div class="thumbimage"><a href="/wiki/File:Pi_y_margall.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Pi_y_margall.jpg/159px-Pi_y_margall.jpg" decoding="async" width="159" height="206" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Pi_y_margall.jpg/239px-Pi_y_margall.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Pi_y_margall.jpg/318px-Pi_y_margall.jpg 2x" data-file-width="332" data-file-height="430" /></a></div><div class="thumbcaption"><a href="/wiki/Francesc_Pi_i_Margall" title="Francesc Pi i Margall">Francesc Pi i Margall</a><div style="clear:both;"></div>(president of the <a href="/wiki/First_Spanish_Republic" title="First Spanish Republic">First Spanish Republic</a>)</div></div></div></div></div>
<p>Two major factors were <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Spain" title="Constitutional Court of Spain">Spain's Constitutional Court's</a> 2010 decision to declare part of the 2006 Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia unconstitutional, as well as the fact that Catalonia contributes 19.49% of the central government's tax revenue, but only receives 14.03% of central government's spending.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Parties that consider themselves either Catalan nationalist or <a href="/wiki/Catalan_independence" class="mw-redirect" title="Catalan independence">independentist</a> have been present in all Catalan governments since 1980. The largest Catalan nationalist party, <a href="/wiki/Convergence_and_Union" title="Convergence and Union">Convergence and Union</a>, ruled Catalonia from 1980 to 2003, and returned to power in the <a href="/wiki/2010_Catalan_regional_election" title="2010 Catalan regional election">2010 election</a>. Between 2003 and 2010, a leftist coalition, composed by the <a href="/wiki/Partit_dels_Socialistes_de_Catalunya" class="mw-redirect" title="Partit dels Socialistes de Catalunya">Catalan Socialists' Party</a>, the pro-independence <a href="/wiki/Republican_Left_of_Catalonia" title="Republican Left of Catalonia">Republican Left of Catalonia</a> and the leftist-environmentalist <a href="/wiki/Iniciativa_per_Catalunya_Verds" class="mw-redirect" title="Iniciativa per Catalunya Verds">Initiative for Catalonia-Greens</a>, implemented policies that widened Catalan autonomy.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2012_Catalonian_parliamentary_election" class="mw-redirect" title="2012 Catalonian parliamentary election">25 November 2012 Catalan parliamentary election</a>, sovereigntist parties supporting a secession referendum gathered 59.01% of the votes and held 87 of the 135 seats in the Catalan Parliament. Parties supporting independence from the rest of Spain obtained 49.12% of the votes and a majority of 74 seats.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Artur_Mas" title="Artur Mas">Artur Mas</a>, then the president of Catalonia, organised early elections that took place on 27 September 2015. In these elections, Convergència and Esquerra Republicana decided to join, and they presented themselves under the coalition named "Junts pel Sí" (in <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">Catalan</a>, "<a href="/wiki/Together_for_Yes" title="Together for Yes">Together for Yes</a>"). "Junts pel Sí" won 62 seats and was the most voted party, and CUP (<a href="/wiki/Candidatura_d%27Unitat_Popular" class="mw-redirect" title="Candidatura d&#39;Unitat Popular">Candidatura d'Unitat Popular</a>, a far-left and independentist party) won another 10, so the sum of all the independentist forces/parties was 72 seats, reaching an absolute majority, but not in number of individual votes, comprising 47,74% of the total.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Statute_of_Autonomy">Statute of Autonomy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Statute of Autonomy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Autonomy_of_Catalonia" title="Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia">Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia</a></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Autonomous_communities_of_Spain" title="Autonomous communities of Spain">Autonomous communities of Spain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nationalities_and_regions_of_Spain" title="Nationalities and regions of Spain">Nationalities and regions of Spain</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg/220px-Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="310" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg/330px-Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg/440px-Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1137" data-file-height="1600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Estatuto_de_Nuria.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The first <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Statute of Catalonia">Statute of Catalonia</a>, 1932</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Autonomy" title="Statute of Autonomy">Statute of Autonomy</a> of Catalonia is the fundamental organic law, second only to the Spanish Constitution from which the Statute originates.
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Constitution_of_1978" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Constitution of 1978">Spanish Constitution of 1978</a> Catalonia, along with the <a href="/wiki/Basque_Country_(autonomous_community)" title="Basque Country (autonomous community)">Basque Country</a> and <a href="/wiki/Galicia_(Spain)" title="Galicia (Spain)">Galicia</a>, was defined as a "<a href="/wiki/Nationalities_and_regions_of_Spain" title="Nationalities and regions of Spain">nationality</a>". The same constitution gave Catalonia the automatic right to autonomy, which resulted in the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Autonomy_of_Catalonia_of_1979" title="Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia of 1979">Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia of 1979</a>.
</p><p>Both the 1979 Statute of Autonomy and the current one, approved in 2006, state that "Catalonia, as a nationality, exercises its self-government constituted as an Autonomous Community in accordance with the Constitution and with the Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia, which is its basic institutional law, always under the law in Spain".<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Preamble of the 2006 Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia states that the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Catalonia" title="Parliament of Catalonia">Parliament of Catalonia</a> has defined Catalonia as a <a href="/wiki/Nation" title="Nation">nation</a>, but that "the Spanish Constitution recognizes Catalonia's national reality as a nationality".<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> While the Statute was approved by and sanctioned by both the Catalan and Spanish parliaments, and later by referendum in Catalonia, it has been subject to a legal challenge by the surrounding autonomous communities of <a href="/wiki/Aragon" title="Aragon">Aragon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Balearic_Islands" title="Balearic Islands">Balearic Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Valencian_Community" title="Valencian Community">Valencia</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> as well as by the conservative <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Party_(Spain)" title="People&#39;s Party (Spain)">People's Party</a>. The objections are based on various issues such as disputed <a href="/wiki/Cultural_heritage" title="Cultural heritage">cultural heritage</a> but, especially, on the Statute's alleged breaches of the principle of "solidarity between regions" in fiscal and educational matters enshrined by the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Constitution_of_1978" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish Constitution of 1978">Constitution</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Spain's <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Spain" title="Constitutional Court of Spain">Constitutional Court</a> assessed the disputed articles and on 28 June 2010, issued its judgment on the principal allegation of unconstitutionality presented by the People's Party in 2006. The judgment granted clear passage to 182 articles of the 223 that make up the fundamental text. The court approved 73 of the 114 articles that the People's Party had contested, while declaring 14 articles unconstitutional in whole or in part and imposing a restrictive interpretation on 27 others.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> The court accepted the specific provision that described Catalonia as a "nation", however ruled that it was a historical and cultural term with no legal weight, and that Spain remained the only nation recognised by the constitution.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Government_and_law">Government and law</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Government and law">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Generalitat_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Generalitat of Catalonia">Generalitat of Catalonia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG/220px-Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG/330px-Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG/440px-Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Parliament_of_Catalunya.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Catalonia" title="Parliament of Catalonia">Parliament of Catalonia</a>, located in <a href="/wiki/Ciutadella_park" class="mw-redirect" title="Ciutadella park">Ciutadella park</a>, Barcelona</div></div></div>
<p>The Catalan Statute of Autonomy establishes that Catalonia is organised politically through the <a href="/wiki/Generalitat_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Generalitat of Catalonia">Generalitat of Catalonia</a> (in Catalan: <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Generalitat de Catalunya</i>), conformed by the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Catalonia" title="Parliament of Catalonia">Parliament</a>, the Presidency of the Generalitat, the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Government of Catalonia">Government</a> or Executive Council and the other institutions created by the Parliament, among them the Ombudsman (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text"><a href="/w/index.php?title=S%C3%ADndic_de_Greuges_(Catalonia)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Síndic de Greuges (Catalonia) (page does not exist)">Síndic de Greuges</a></i>), the Office of Auditors (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Sindicatura de Comptes</i>) or the Council for Statutory Guarantees (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Consell de Garanties Estatutàries</i>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Casa_generalitat_web.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Casa_generalitat_web.jpg/220px-Casa_generalitat_web.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Casa_generalitat_web.jpg/330px-Casa_generalitat_web.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Casa_generalitat_web.jpg/440px-Casa_generalitat_web.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="1333" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Casa_generalitat_web.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text"><a href="/wiki/Palau_de_la_Generalitat_de_Catalunya" title="Palau de la Generalitat de Catalunya">Palau de la Generalitat de Catalunya</a></i>, Barcelona, seat of the Government and the Presidency of Catalonia</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg/220px-Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="134" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg/330px-Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg/440px-Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4000" data-file-height="2445" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Govern_de_Catalunya_primera_reuni%C3%B3_2018.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Torra_Government" title="Torra Government">Government of Catalonia (2018–)</a>. Quim Torra, President of the Generalitat, is in the background, at the center; <a href="/wiki/Pere_Aragon%C3%A8s" title="Pere Aragonès">Pere Aragonès</a>, the Vice-president, on his right from his point of view</div></div></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Legislature">Legislature</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Legislature">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The Parliament of Catalonia (in Catalan: <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Parlament de Catalunya</i>) is the legislative body of the Generalitat and represents the citizens of Catalonia. It is elected every four years by <a href="/wiki/Universal_suffrage" title="Universal suffrage">universal suffrage</a>, and it has powers to legislate in different matters such as education, health, culture, internal institutional and territorial organization, election and control of the president of the Generalitat and the Government, budget and other affairs, according with the Statute of Autonomy. The last Catalan election was held on 21 December 2017, and its current president is <a href="/wiki/Roger_Torrent" title="Roger Torrent">Roger Torrent</a>, incumbent since January 2018.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Presidency">Presidency</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Presidency">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_Generalitat_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="President of the Generalitat of Catalonia">president of the Generalitat of Catalonia</a> (in Catalan: <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">president de la Generalitat de Catalunya</i>) is the highest representative of Catalonia, and is also responsible of leading the government's action. Since the restoration of the Generalitat on the return of democracy in Spain, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_the_Generalitat_de_Catalunya" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of the Generalitat de Catalunya">presidents of Catalonia</a> have been <a href="/wiki/Josep_Tarradellas" title="Josep Tarradellas">Josep Tarradellas</a> (1977–1980, president in exile since 1954), <a href="/wiki/Jordi_Pujol" title="Jordi Pujol">Jordi Pujol</a> (1980–2003), <a href="/wiki/Pasqual_Maragall" title="Pasqual Maragall">Pasqual Maragall</a> (2003–2006), <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Montilla" title="José Montilla">José Montilla</a> (2006–2010), <a href="/wiki/Artur_Mas" title="Artur Mas">Artur Mas</a> (2010–2016), <a href="/wiki/Carles_Puigdemont" title="Carles Puigdemont">Carles Puigdemont</a> (2016&#8211;2017) and, after the imposition of direct rule from government of Spain<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>, <a href="/wiki/Quim_Torra" title="Quim Torra">Quim Torra</a> (2018–).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Executive">Executive</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Executive">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Executive_Council_of_Catalonia" title="Executive Council of Catalonia">Executive Council</a> (in Catalan: <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Consell Executiu</i>) or Government (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Govern</i>), is the body responsible of the government of the Generalitat, it holds executive and regulatory power. It comprises the president of the Generalitat, the <a href="/wiki/List_of_First_Ministers_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="List of First Ministers of Catalonia">First Minister</a> (or the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Vice_Presidents_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Vice Presidents of Catalonia">Vice President</a>) and the Ministers (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">consellers</i>). Its seat is the <a href="/wiki/Palau_de_la_Generalitat_de_Catalunya" title="Palau de la Generalitat de Catalunya">Palau de la Generalitat</a>, in Barcelona.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Security_forces_and_Justice">Security forces and Justice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Security forces and Justice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Mossos_d%27Esquadra" title="Mossos d&#39;Esquadra">Mossos d'Esquadra</a></div>
<p>Catalonia has its own police force, the <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text"><a href="/wiki/Mossos_d%27Esquadra" title="Mossos d&#39;Esquadra">Mossos d'Esquadra</a></i> (officially called <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Mossos d'Esquadra-Policia de la Generalitat de Catalunya</i>), whose origins date back to the 18th century. Since 1980 they have been under the command of the Generalitat, and since 1994 they have expanded in number in order to replace the national <a href="/wiki/Civil_Guard_(Spain)" title="Civil Guard (Spain)">Civil Guard</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Police_Corps" title="National Police Corps">National Police Corps</a>, which report directly to the Homeland Department of Spain. The national bodies retain personnel within Catalonia to exercise functions of national scope such as overseeing ports, airports, coasts, international borders, custom offices, the identification of documents and arms control, immigration control, terrorism prevention, arms trafficking prevention, amongst others.
</p><p>Most of the justice system is administered by national judicial institutions, the highest body and last judicial instance in the Catalan jurisdiction, integrating the Spanish judiciary, is the <a href="/wiki/High_Court_of_Justice_of_Catalonia" title="High Court of Justice of Catalonia">High Court of Justice of Catalonia</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Criminal_justice" title="Criminal justice">criminal justice</a> system is uniform throughout Spain, while <a href="/wiki/Civil_law_(legal_system)" title="Civil law (legal system)">civil law</a> is administered separately within Catalonia. The civil laws that are subject to autonomous legislation have been codified in the <a href="/wiki/Civil_Code_of_Catalonia" title="Civil Code of Catalonia">Civil Code of Catalonia</a> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Codi civil de Catalunya</i>) since 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Navarre" title="Navarre">Navarre</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Basque_Country_(autonomous_community)" title="Basque Country (autonomous community)">Basque Country</a> and Catalonia are the Spanish communities with the highest degree of autonomy in terms of <a href="/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency" title="Law enforcement agency">law enforcement</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_divisions">Administrative divisions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Administrative divisions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:322px;"><a href="/wiki/File:CatMCVPtoponims.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/CatMCVPtoponims.svg/320px-CatMCVPtoponims.svg.png" decoding="async" width="320" height="310" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/CatMCVPtoponims.svg/480px-CatMCVPtoponims.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/af/CatMCVPtoponims.svg/640px-CatMCVPtoponims.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="775" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:CatMCVPtoponims.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Administrative divisions of Catalonia</div></div></div>
<p>Catalonia is organised territorially into <a href="/wiki/Province" title="Province">provinces</a>, further subdivided into <a href="/wiki/Comarca" title="Comarca">comarques</a> and <a href="/wiki/Municipality" title="Municipality">municipalities</a>. The 2006 Statute of Autonomy of Catalonia establishes the administrative organisation of three local authorities: <a href="/wiki/Vegueria" title="Vegueria">vegueries</a>, comarques, and municipalities.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Provinces">Provinces</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Provinces">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Provinces_of_Spain" title="Provinces of Spain">Provinces of Spain</a></div>
<p>Catalonia is divided administratively into four provinces, the governing body of which is the Provincial Deputation (Catalan: <i lang="ca">Diputació Provincial</i>, Spanish: <i lang="es">Diputación Provincial</i>). The four provinces and their populations are:<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Province_of_Barcelona" title="Province of Barcelona">Province of Barcelona</a>: 5,507,813 population</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Province_of_Girona" title="Province of Girona">Province of Girona</a>: 752,026 population</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Province_of_Lleida" title="Province of Lleida">Province of Lleida</a>: 439,253 population</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Province_of_Tarragona" title="Province of Tarragona">Province of Tarragona</a>: 805,789 population</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Comarques">Comarques</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Comarques">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Comarques_of_Catalonia" title="Comarques of Catalonia">Comarques of Catalonia</a></div>
<p>Comarques (singular: "comarca") are entities composed by the municipalities to manage their responsibilities and services. The current regional division has its roots in a decree of the Generalitat de Catalunya of 1936, in effect until 1939, when it was suppressed by Franco. In 1987 the Government adopted the territorial division again and in 1988 three new comarques were added (<a href="/wiki/Alta_Ribagor%C3%A7a" title="Alta Ribagorça">Alta Ribagorça</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pla_d%27Urgell" title="Pla d&#39;Urgell">Pla d'Urgell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pla_de_l%27Estany" title="Pla de l&#39;Estany">Pla de l'Estany</a>), and in 2015 was created another comarca, the <a href="/wiki/Moian%C3%A8s" title="Moianès">Moianès</a>. At present there are 41. Every comarca is administered by a <a href="/wiki/Comarcal_council" title="Comarcal council">comarcal council</a> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">consell comarcal</i>).
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Val_d%27Aran" title="Val d&#39;Aran">Val d'Aran</a> (Aran Valley), until 2015 considered as a comarca, is officially defined today as "unique territorial entity", has a special status and its autonomous government is named <i lang="oc" title="Occitan language text"><a href="/wiki/Conselh_Generau_d%27Aran" title="Conselh Generau d&#39;Aran">Conselh Generau d'Aran</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Municipalities">Municipalities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Municipalities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Catalonia" title="Municipalities of Catalonia">Municipalities of Catalonia</a></div>
<p>There are at present 948 municipalities (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">municipis</i>) in Catalonia. Each municipality is run by a council (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">ajuntament</i>) elected every four years by the residents in local elections. The council consists of a number of members (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">regidors</i>) depending on population, who elect the <a href="/wiki/Mayor" title="Mayor">mayor</a> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">alcalde</i> or <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">batlle</i>). Its seat is the <a href="/wiki/Town_hall" class="mw-redirect" title="Town hall">town hall</a> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">ajuntament</i>, <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">casa de la ciutat</i> or <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">casa de la vila</i>).
</p>
