<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vegueries">Vegueries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Vegueries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Vegueries_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Vegueries of Catalonia">Vegueries of Catalonia</a></div>
<p>The <i>vegueria</i> is a new type of division defined as a specific territorial area for the exercise of government and inter-local cooperation with legal personality. The current Statute of Autonomy states vegueries are intended to supersede provinces in Catalonia, and take over many of functions of the comarques.
</p><p>The territorial plan of Catalonia (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Pla territorial general de Catalunya</i>) provided six general functional areas,<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> but was amended by Law 24/2001, of 31 December, recognizing the <a href="/wiki/Alt_Pirineu_i_Aran" title="Alt Pirineu i Aran">Alt Pirineu i Aran</a> as a new functional area differentiated of Ponent.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> On 14 July 2010 the Catalan Parliament approved the creation of the functional area of the <a href="/wiki/Pened%C3%A8s" title="Penedès">Penedès</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alt_Pirineu_i_Aran" title="Alt Pirineu i Aran">Alt Pirineu i Aran</a>: <a href="/wiki/Alta_Ribagor%C3%A7a" title="Alta Ribagorça">Alta Ribagorça</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alt_Urgell" title="Alt Urgell">Alt Urgell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cerdanya" title="Cerdanya">Cerdanya</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pallars_Juss%C3%A0" title="Pallars Jussà">Pallars Jussà</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pallars_Sobir%C3%A0" title="Pallars Sobirà">Pallars Sobirà</a> and Val d'Aran.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%80mbit_Metropolit%C3%A0_de_Barcelona" class="mw-redirect" title="Àmbit Metropolità de Barcelona">Àmbit Metropolità de Barcelona</a>: <a href="/wiki/Baix_Llobregat" title="Baix Llobregat">Baix Llobregat</a>, Barcelonès, <a href="/wiki/Garraf" title="Garraf">Garraf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maresme" title="Maresme">Maresme</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vall%C3%A8s_Oriental" title="Vallès Oriental">Vallès Oriental</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vall%C3%A8s_Occidental" title="Vallès Occidental">Vallès Occidental</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Camp_de_Tarragona" title="Camp de Tarragona">Camp de Tarragona</a>: <a href="/wiki/Tarragon%C3%A8s" title="Tarragonès">Tarragonès</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alt_Camp" title="Alt Camp">Alt Camp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Baix_Camp" title="Baix Camp">Baix Camp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Conca_de_Barber%C3%A0" title="Conca de Barberà">Conca de Barberà</a> and <a href="/wiki/Priorat" title="Priorat">Priorat</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Comarques_gironines" class="mw-redirect" title="Comarques gironines">Comarques gironines</a>: <a href="/wiki/Alt_Empord%C3%A0" title="Alt Empordà">Alt Empordà</a>, <a href="/wiki/Baix_Empord%C3%A0" title="Baix Empordà">Baix Empordà</a>, <a href="/wiki/Garrotxa" title="Garrotxa">Garrotxa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Giron%C3%A8s" title="Gironès">Gironès</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pla_de_l%27Estany" title="Pla de l&#39;Estany">Pla de l'Estany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Selva" title="Selva">La Selva</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ripoll%C3%A8s" title="Ripollès">Ripollès</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Comarques_Centrals" title="Comarques Centrals">Comarques centrals</a>: <a href="/wiki/Anoia" title="Anoia">Anoia</a> (8 municipalities of 33), <a href="/wiki/Bages" title="Bages">Bages</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bergued%C3%A0" title="Berguedà">Berguedà</a>, <a href="/wiki/Osona" title="Osona">Osona</a> and <a href="/wiki/Solson%C3%A8s" title="Solsonès">Solsonès</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pened%C3%A8s" title="Penedès">Penedès</a>: <a href="/wiki/Alt_Pened%C3%A8s" title="Alt Penedès">Alt Penedès</a>, <a href="/wiki/Baix_Pened%C3%A8s" title="Baix Penedès">Baix Penedès</a>, Anoia (25 municipalities of 33) and <a href="/wiki/Garraf" title="Garraf">Garraf</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ponent" title="Ponent">Ponent</a>: <a href="/wiki/Garrigues_(comarca)" title="Garrigues (comarca)">Garrigues</a>, <a href="/wiki/Noguera_(comarca)" title="Noguera (comarca)">Noguera</a>, <a href="/wiki/Segarra" title="Segarra">Segarra</a>, <a href="/wiki/Segri%C3%A0" title="Segrià">Segrià</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pla_d%27Urgell" title="Pla d&#39;Urgell">Pla d'Urgell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Urgell" title="Urgell">Urgell</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Terres_de_l%27Ebre" title="Terres de l&#39;Ebre">Terres de l'Ebre</a>: <a href="/wiki/Baix_Ebre" title="Baix Ebre">Baix Ebre</a>, <a href="/wiki/Montsi%C3%A0" title="Montsià">Montsià</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ribera_d%27Ebre" title="Ribera d&#39;Ebre">Ribera d'Ebre</a> and <a href="/wiki/Terra_Alta_(comarca)" title="Terra Alta (comarca)">Terra Alta</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_Spain" title="Economy of Spain">Economy of Spain</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona,_Segri%C3%A0.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona%2C_Segri%C3%A0.jpg/220px-Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona%2C_Segri%C3%A0.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona%2C_Segri%C3%A0.jpg/330px-Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona%2C_Segri%C3%A0.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona%2C_Segri%C3%A0.jpg/440px-Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona%2C_Segri%C3%A0.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6000" data-file-height="4000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Camps_de_Presseguers_a_Aitona,_Segri%C3%A0.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Peach fields in <a href="/wiki/Aitona" title="Aitona">Aitona</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG/220px-Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG/330px-Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG/440px-Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG 2x" data-file-width="4592" data-file-height="3056" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Strand_Santa_Cristina.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Costa_Brava" title="Costa Brava">Costa Brava</a> beach. <a href="/wiki/Tourism_in_Spain" title="Tourism in Spain">Tourism</a> plays an important role in the Catalan economy.</div></div></div>
<p>A highly industrialized land, the nominal <a href="/wiki/Gross_domestic_product" title="Gross domestic product">GDP</a> of Catalonia in 2014 was €200 billion (usually the highest in Spain) and the per capita GDP was €27,000 ($30,000), behind <a href="/wiki/Madrid_(autonomous_community)" class="mw-redirect" title="Madrid (autonomous community)">Madrid</a> (€31,000), the Basque Country (€30,000), and <a href="/wiki/Navarre" title="Navarre">Navarre</a> (€28,000).<sup id="cite_ref-ine.es_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ine.es-111">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> In that year, the GDP growth was 1.4%.<sup id="cite_ref-ine.es_111-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ine.es-111">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> In recent years there has been a negative net relocation rate of companies based in Catalonia moving to other autonomous communities of Spain. In 2014, for example, Catalonia lost 987 companies to other parts of Spain (mainly Madrid), gaining 602 new ones from the rest of the country.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Catalonia's long-term credit rating is BB (Non-Investment Grade) according to <a href="/wiki/Standard_%26_Poor%27s" title="Standard &amp; Poor&#39;s">Standard &amp; Poor's</a>, Ba2 (Non-Investment Grade) according to <a href="/wiki/Moody%27s" class="mw-redirect" title="Moody&#39;s">Moody's</a>, and BBB- (Low Investment Grade) according to <a href="/wiki/Fitch_Ratings" title="Fitch Ratings">Fitch Ratings</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-agency-ratings_115-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-agency-ratings-115">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> Catalonia's rating is tied for worst with between 1 and 5 other autonomous communities of Spain, depending on the rating agency.<sup id="cite_ref-agency-ratings_115-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-agency-ratings-115">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the context of the <a href="/wiki/Financial_crisis_of_2007%E2%80%932008" title="Financial crisis of 2007–2008">financial crisis of 2007–2008</a>, Catalonia was expected to suffer a <a href="/wiki/Recession" title="Recession">recession</a> amounting to almost a 2% contraction of its regional GDP in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Catalonia's debt in 2012 was the highest of all Spain's autonomous communities,<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> reaching €13,476 million, i.e. 38% of the total debt of the 17 autonomous communities,<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> but in recent years its economy recovered a positive evolution and the GDP grew a 3.3% in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg/220px-Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg/330px-Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/12/Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg/440px-Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1950" data-file-height="1300" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pol%C3%ADgon_Industrial_Aquiberia_-_panoramio.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Industrial park in <a href="/wiki/Castellbisbal" title="Castellbisbal">Castellbisbal</a></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png/220px-Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="105" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png/330px-Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png/440px-Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="383" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Tarragona_Poligon_Nord.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Factories, <a href="/wiki/La_Pobla_de_Mafumet" title="La Pobla de Mafumet">La Pobla de Mafumet</a>, Tarragona</div></div></div>
<p>Catalonia is amongst the <a href="/wiki/List_of_country_subdivisions_by_GDP_over_100_billion_US_dollars" class="mw-redirect" title="List of country subdivisions by GDP over 100 billion US dollars">List of country subdivisions by GDP over 100 billion US dollars</a> and is a member of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Motors_for_Europe" title="Four Motors for Europe">Four Motors for Europe</a> organisation.
</p><p>The distribution of sectors is as follows:<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Primary_sector_of_industry" class="mw-redirect" title="Primary sector of industry">Primary sector</a>: 3%. The amount of land devoted to agricultural use is 33%.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Secondary_sector_of_industry" class="mw-redirect" title="Secondary sector of industry">Secondary sector</a>: 37% (compared to Spain's 29%)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tertiary_sector_of_industry" class="mw-redirect" title="Tertiary sector of industry">Tertiary sector</a>: 60% (compared to Spain's 67%)</li></ul>
<p>The main tourist destinations in Catalonia are the city of Barcelona, the beaches of the Costa Brava in <a href="/wiki/Girona" title="Girona">Girona</a>, the beaches of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Costa_del_Maresme&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Costa del Maresme (page does not exist)">Costa del Maresme</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Costa_del_Garraf&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Costa del Garraf (page does not exist)">Costa del Garraf</a> from <a href="/wiki/Malgrat_de_Mar" title="Malgrat de Mar">Malgrat de Mar</a> to <a href="/wiki/Vilanova_i_la_Geltr%C3%BA" title="Vilanova i la Geltrú">Vilanova i la Geltrú</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Costa_Daurada" title="Costa Daurada">Costa Daurada</a> in Tarragona. In the High Pyrenees there are several ski resorts, near <a href="/wiki/Lleida" title="Lleida">Lleida</a>. On 1 November 2012, Catalonia started charging a tourist tax.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> The revenue is used to promote tourism, and to maintain and upgrade tourism-related infrastructure.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg/220px-Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg/330px-Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg/440px-Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1360" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Sabadell_-_Eix_Maci%C3%A0.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Eix Macià, <a href="/wiki/Sabadell" title="Sabadell">Sabadell</a></div></div></div>
<p>Many <a href="/wiki/Savings_bank" title="Savings bank">savings banks</a> are based in Catalonia, with 10 of the 46 Spanish savings banks having headquarters in the region. This list includes Europe's premier savings bank, <a href="/wiki/La_Caixa" title="La Caixa">La Caixa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> The first <a href="/wiki/Private_bank" title="Private bank">private bank</a> in Catalonia is <a href="/wiki/Banc_Sabadell" class="mw-redirect" title="Banc Sabadell">Banc Sabadell</a>, ranked fourth among all Spanish private banks.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The stock market of Barcelona, which in 2016 had a volume of around €152 billion, is the second largest of Spain after Madrid, and <a href="/wiki/Fira_de_Barcelona" title="Fira de Barcelona">Fira de Barcelona</a> organizes international exhibitions and congresses to do with different sectors of the economy.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The main economic cost for the Catalan families is the purchase of a home. According to data from the Society of Appraisal on 31 December 2005 Catalonia is, after Madrid, the second most expensive region in Spain for housing: 3,397&#160;€/m<sup>2</sup> on average (see <a href="/wiki/Spanish_property_bubble" title="Spanish property bubble">Spanish property bubble</a>).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Unemployment">Unemployment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Unemployment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The unemployment rate stood at 11.5% in 2018 and was lower than the national average.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Transport">Transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Airports">Airports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Airports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:TorreControElPrat.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/TorreControElPrat.jpg/220px-TorreControElPrat.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="185" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/TorreControElPrat.jpg/330px-TorreControElPrat.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/TorreControElPrat.jpg/440px-TorreControElPrat.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2126" data-file-height="1789" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:TorreControElPrat.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Barcelona_El_Prat_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Barcelona El Prat Airport">Barcelona Airport</a> tower</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_airports_in_Catalonia" title="List of airports in Catalonia">List of airports in Catalonia</a></div>
<p>Airports in Catalonia are owned and operated by <a href="/wiki/Aena" class="mw-redirect" title="Aena">Aena</a> (a <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Spain" title="Government of Spain">Spanish Government</a> entity) except two airports in Lleida which are operated by <a href="/wiki/Aeroports_de_Catalunya" title="Aeroports de Catalunya">Aeroports de Catalunya</a> (an entity belonging to the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Catalonia" class="mw-redirect" title="Government of Catalonia">Government of Catalonia</a>).
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Barcelona_El_Prat_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Barcelona El Prat Airport">Barcelona El Prat Airport</a> (Aena)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Girona-Costa_Brava_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Girona-Costa Brava Airport">Girona-Costa Brava Airport</a> (Aena)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Reus_Airport" title="Reus Airport">Reus Airport</a> (Aena)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lleida-Alguaire_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Lleida-Alguaire Airport">Lleida-Alguaire Airport</a> (Aeroports de Catalunya)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sabadell_Airport" title="Sabadell Airport">Sabadell Airport</a> (Aena)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/La_Seu_d%27Urgell_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="La Seu d&#39;Urgell Airport">La Seu d'Urgell Airport</a> (Aeroports de Catalunya)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ports">Ports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Ports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_ports_in_Spain" title="List of ports in Spain">List of ports in Spain</a></div>
<p>Since the Middle Ages, Catalonia has been well integrated into international maritime networks. The <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Barcelona" title="Port of Barcelona">port of Barcelona</a> (owned and operated by <i lang="es" title="Spanish language text"><a href="https://es.wikipedia.org/wiki/Puertos_del_Estado" class="extiw" title="es:Puertos del Estado">Puertos del Estado</a></i>, a Spanish Government entity) is an industrial, commercial and tourist port of worldwide importance. With 1,950,000 <a href="/wiki/Twenty-foot_equivalent_unit" title="Twenty-foot equivalent unit">TEUs</a> in 2015, it is the first container port in Catalonia, the third in Spain after Valencia and <a href="/wiki/Algeciras" title="Algeciras">Algeciras</a> in Andalusia, the 9th in the Mediterranean Sea, the 14th in Europe and the 68th in the world. It is sixth largest cruise port in the world, the first in Europe and the Mediterranean with 2,364,292 passengers in 2014. The ports of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Port_of_Tarragona&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Port of Tarragona (page does not exist)">Tarragona</a> (owned and operated by Puertos del Estado) in the southwest and <a href="/wiki/Palam%C3%B3s" title="Palamós">Palamós</a> near Girona at northeast are much more modest. The port of Palamós and the other ports in Catalonia (26) are operated and administered by <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text"><a href="https://ca.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ports_de_la_Generalitat" class="extiw" title="ca:Ports de la Generalitat">Ports de la Generalitat</a></i>, a Catalan Government entity.
</p><p>The development of these infrastructures, resulting from the topography and history of the Catalan territory, responds strongly to the administrative and political organization of this autonomous community.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Roads">Roads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Roads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_primary_highways_in_Catalonia" title="List of primary highways in Catalonia">List of primary highways in Catalonia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Autopista_C-16.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Autopista_C-16.jpg/220px-Autopista_C-16.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="150" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Autopista_C-16.jpg/330px-Autopista_C-16.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Autopista_C-16.jpg/440px-Autopista_C-16.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1022" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Autopista_C-16.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Autov%C3%ADa_C-16" class="mw-redirect" title="Autovía C-16">Autovia C-16</a> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Eix del Llobregat</i>)</div></div></div>
<p>There are 12,000 kilometres (7,500&#160;mi) of roads throughout Catalonia.
</p><p>The principal highways are <span style="background: #009; color: white"><b>&#160;AP-7&#160;</b></span> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Autopista de la Mediterrània</i>) and <span style="background: #009; color: white"><b>&#160;A-7&#160;</b></span> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Autovia de la Mediterrània</i>). They follow the coast from the <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French border</a> to <a href="/wiki/Valencian_Community" title="Valencian Community">Valencia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Region_of_Murcia" title="Region of Murcia">Murcia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andalusia" title="Andalusia">Andalusia</a>. The main roads generally radiate from Barcelona. The <span style="background: #009; color: white"><b>&#160;AP-2&#160;</b></span> <a href="/wiki/File:Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg" class="image"><img alt="Spain traffic signal r200.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg/16px-Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg/24px-Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg/32px-Spain_traffic_signal_r200.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="48" data-file-height="48" /></a> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Autopista del Nord-est</i>) and <span style="background: #009; color: white"><b>&#160;A-2&#160;</b></span> (<i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text">Autovia del Nord-est</i>) connect inland and onward to Madrid.
</p><p>Other major roads are:
</p>

<td><a href="/wiki/Argentona" title="Argentona">Argentona</a>-<a href="/wiki/La_Roca_del_Vall%C3%A8s" title="La Roca del Vallès">La Roca del Vallès</a>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Public-own roads in Catalonia are either managed by the autonomous government of Catalonia (e.g., <span style="background: red; color: white"><b>&#160;C-&#160;</b></span> roads) or the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_government" class="mw-redirect" title="Spanish government">Spanish government</a> (e.g., <span style="background: #009; color: white"><b>&#160;AP-&#160;</b></span>, <span style="background: #009; color: white"><b>&#160;A-&#160;</b></span>, <span style="background: red; color: white"><b>&#160;N-&#160;</b></span> roads).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Railways">Railways</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Railways">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Rail_transport_in_Catalonia" title="Rail transport in Catalonia">Rail transport in Catalonia</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:RN103007TarJPVL.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/RN103007TarJPVL.JPG/220px-RN103007TarJPVL.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/RN103007TarJPVL.JPG/330px-RN103007TarJPVL.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c9/RN103007TarJPVL.JPG/440px-RN103007TarJPVL.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="670" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:RN103007TarJPVL.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/AVE" title="AVE">High-speed train (AVE)</a> at <a href="/wiki/Camp_de_Tarragona" title="Camp de Tarragona">Camp de Tarragona</a></div></div></div>
<p>Catalonia saw the first railway construction in the <a href="/wiki/Iberian_Peninsula" title="Iberian Peninsula">Iberian Peninsula</a> in 1848, linking Barcelona with <a href="/wiki/Matar%C3%B3" title="Mataró">Mataró</a>. Given the topography most lines radiate from Barcelona. The city has both suburban and inter-city services. The main east coast line runs through the province connecting with the <a href="/wiki/SNCF" title="SNCF">SNCF</a> (French Railways) at <a href="/wiki/Portbou" title="Portbou">Portbou</a> on the coast.
</p><p>There are two publicly owned railway companies operating in Catalonia: the Catalan <a href="/wiki/Ferrocarrils_de_la_Generalitat_de_Catalunya" title="Ferrocarrils de la Generalitat de Catalunya">FGC</a> that operates commuter and regional services, and the Spanish national <a href="/wiki/RENFE" class="mw-redirect" title="RENFE">RENFE</a> that operates long-distance and high-speed rail services (AVE and Avant) and the main commuter and regional service <i lang="ca" title="Catalan language text"><a href="/wiki/Rodalies_de_Catalunya" title="Rodalies de Catalunya">Rodalies de Catalunya</a></i>, administered by the Catalan government since 2010.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/High-speed_rail" title="High-speed rail">High-speed rail</a> (<a href="/wiki/AVE" title="AVE">AVE</a>) services from <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a> currently reach Lleida, Tarragona and Barcelona. The official opening between Barcelona and Madrid took place 20 February 2008. The journey between Barcelona and Madrid now takes about two-and-a-half hours. A connection to the <a href="/wiki/High-speed_rail_in_France#Network" title="High-speed rail in France">French high-speed TGV network</a> has been completed (called the <a href="/wiki/Perpignan%E2%80%93Barcelona_high-speed_rail_line" title="Perpignan–Barcelona high-speed rail line">Perpignan–Barcelona high-speed rail line</a>) and the Spanish AVE service began commercial services on the line 9 January 2013, later offering services to Marseille on their high speed network.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_127-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-127">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> This was shortly followed by the commencement of commercial service by the French TGV on 17 January 2013, leading to an average travel time on the <a href="/wiki/List_of_TGV_services#International" title="List of TGV services">Paris-Barcelona TGV</a> route of 7h 42m.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_127-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-127">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> This new line passes through <a href="/wiki/Girona" title="Girona">Girona</a> and <a href="/wiki/Figueres" title="Figueres">Figueres</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Perthus_Tunnel" title="Perthus Tunnel">tunnel</a> through the Pyrenees.
</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>

style="text-align:right;padding:1px">3,925,779</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+21.2%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">1970</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">5,122,567</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+30.5%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">1981</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">5,949,829</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+16.1%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px;border-bottom:1px solid #bbbbbb">1990</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px;border-bottom:1px solid #bbbbbb">6,062,273</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px;border-bottom:1px solid #bbbbbb">+1.9%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">2000</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">6,174,547</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+1.9%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">2010</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">7,462,044</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">+20.9%</td></tr><tr><th style="text-align:center;padding:1px">2017</th><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">7,441,176</td><td style="text-align:right;padding:1px">−0.3%</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3" style="border-top:1px solid black;font-size:85%;text-align:left">Source: <a href="/wiki/Instituto_Nacional_de_Estad%C3%ADstica_(Spain)" title="Instituto Nacional de Estadística (Spain)">INE</a></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>As of 2017, the official population of Catalonia was 7,522,596.<sup id="cite_ref-popcat_129-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-popcat-129">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> 1,194,947 residents did not have Spanish citizenship, accounting for about 16% of the population.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Urban_Region_of_Barcelona" class="mw-redirect" title="Urban Region of Barcelona">Urban Region of Barcelona</a> includes 5,217,864 people and covers an area of 2,268&#160;km<sup>2</sup> (876&#160;sq&#160;mi). The metropolitan area of the Urban Region includes cities such as <a href="/wiki/L%27Hospitalet_de_Llobregat" title="L&#39;Hospitalet de Llobregat">L'Hospitalet de Llobregat</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sabadell" title="Sabadell">Sabadell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Terrassa" title="Terrassa">Terrassa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Badalona" title="Badalona">Badalona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Santa_Coloma_de_Gramenet" title="Santa Coloma de Gramenet">Santa Coloma de Gramenet</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cornell%C3%A0_de_Llobregat" title="Cornellà de Llobregat">Cornellà de Llobregat</a>.
</p><p>In 1900, the population of Catalonia was 1,966,382 people and in 1970 it was 5,122,567.<sup id="cite_ref-popcat_129-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-popcat-129">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> The sizeable increase of the population was due to the demographic boom in Spain during the 60s and early 70s<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> as well as in consequence of large-scale internal migration from the rural economically weak regions to its more prospering industrial cities. In Catalonia that wave of internal migration arrived from several regions of Spain, especially from <a href="/wiki/Andalusia" title="Andalusia">Andalusia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Region_of_Murcia" title="Region of Murcia">Murcia</a><sup id="cite_ref-REUTCATPOP_132-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-REUTCATPOP-132">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Extremadura" title="Extremadura">Extremadura</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Immigrants from other countries settled in Catalonia since the 1990s;<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> a large percentage comes from <a href="/wiki/Africa" title="Africa">Africa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Latin_America" title="Latin America">Latin America</a> and <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Europe" title="Eastern Europe">Eastern Europe</a>, and smaller numbers from <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Southern_Europe" title="Southern Europe">Southern Europe</a>, often settling in urban centers such as Barcelona and industrial areas.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> In 2017, Catalonia had 1,194,497 foreign residents (15.9% of the total population) with non-Spanish ID cards, without including those who acquired the Spanish citizenship.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">Religion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Religion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_Catalonia" title="Religion in Catalonia">Religion in Catalonia</a></div>

</div>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<p>Religion in Catalonia (2016)<sup id="cite_ref-Barometer2016_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barometer2016-138">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:DarkOrchid; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic Church</a> (58.0%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:DodgerBlue; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Protestantism" title="Protestantism">Protestantism</a> (3.0%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Orchid; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Orthodox_Church" class="mw-redirect" title="Orthodox Church">Orthodox Church</a> (0.9%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Turquoise; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Jehovah%27s_Witnesses" title="Jehovah&#39;s Witnesses">Jehovah's Witnesses</a> (0.6%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:DarkGrey; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Atheism" title="Atheism">Atheism</a> (16.0%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Honeydew; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Agnosticism" title="Agnosticism">Agnosticism</a> (11.9%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Green; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Islam" title="Islam">Islam</a> (4.8%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Yellow; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Buddhism" title="Buddhism">Buddhism</a> (1.3%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Red; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Other religions (2.4%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Black; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;No answer/do not know (1.1%)</div>
</div>
</div></div>
<p>Historically, all the Catalan population was <a href="/wiki/Christianity" title="Christianity">Christian</a>, specifically <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church_in_Spain" title="Catholic Church in Spain">Catholic</a>, but since the 1980s there has been a trend of decline of Christianity and parallel growth of <a href="/wiki/Irreligion" title="Irreligion">irreligion</a> (including stances of <a href="/wiki/Atheism" title="Atheism">atheism</a> and <a href="/wiki/Agnosticism" title="Agnosticism">agnosticism</a>) and other religions. According to the most recent study sponsored by the <a href="/wiki/Generalitat_de_Catalunya" title="Generalitat de Catalunya">government of Catalonia</a>, as of 2016, 61.9% of the Catalans identify as Christians, up from 56.5% in 2014,<sup id="cite_ref-Barometer20142_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barometer20142-139">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> of whom 58.0% Catholics, 3.0% <a href="/wiki/Protestantism" title="Protestantism">Protestants</a> and <a href="/wiki/Evangelicalism" title="Evangelicalism">Evangelicals</a>, 0.9% <a href="/wiki/Orthodox_Christian" class="mw-redirect" title="Orthodox Christian">Orthodox Christians</a> and 0.6% <a href="/wiki/Jehovah%27s_Witnesses" title="Jehovah&#39;s Witnesses">Jehovah's Witnesses</a>. At the same time, 16.0% of the population identify as <a href="/wiki/Atheism" title="Atheism">atheists</a>, 11.9% as <a href="/wiki/Agnosticism" title="Agnosticism">agnostics</a>, 4.8% as <a href="/wiki/Muslims" title="Muslims">Muslims</a>, 1.3% as <a href="/wiki/Buddhism" title="Buddhism">Buddhists</a>, and a further 2.4% as being of other religions.<sup id="cite_ref-Barometer2016_138-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barometer2016-138">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">Languages</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Catalonia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Languages">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Languages_of_Catalonia" title="Languages of Catalonia">Languages of Catalonia</a></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">Catalan language</a>, <a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish language</a>, <a href="/wiki/Occitan_language" title="Occitan language">Occitan language</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Catalan_Sign_Language" title="Catalan Sign Language">Catalan Sign Language</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Paisos_catalans.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Paisos_catalans.svg/220px-Paisos_catalans.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Paisos_catalans.svg/330px-Paisos_catalans.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Paisos_catalans.svg/440px-Paisos_catalans.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1164" data-file-height="1164" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Paisos_catalans.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">Catalan</a>-speaking regions of Europe</div></div></div>
<p>According to the linguistic census held by the Government of Catalonia in 2013, Spanish is the most spoken language in Catalonia (46.53% claim Spanish as "their own language"), followed by <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">Catalan</a> (37.26% claim Catalan as "their own language"). In everyday use, 11.95% of the population claim to use both languages equally, whereas 45.92% mainly use Spanish and 35.54% mainly use Catalan. There is a significant difference between the <a href="/wiki/Barcelona_metropolitan_area" title="Barcelona metropolitan area">Barcelona metropolitan area</a> (and, to a lesser extent, the <a href="/wiki/Camp_de_Tarragona" title="Camp de Tarragona">Tarragona area</a>), where Spanish is more spoken than Catalan, and the more rural and small town areas, where Catalan clearly prevails over Spanish.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Originating in the historic territory of Catalonia, <a href="/wiki/Catalan_language" title="Catalan language">Catalan</a> has enjoyed special status since the approval of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Autonomy_of_1979" class="mw-redirect" title="Statute of Autonomy of 1979">Statute of Autonomy of 1979</a> which declares it to be "Catalonia's own language",<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> a term which signifies a language given special legal status within a Spanish territory, or which is historically spoken within a given region. The other languages with official status are Spanish, which has official status throughout Spain, and Aranese Occitan, which enjoys co-official status with Catalan and Spanish in the Val d'Aran.
</p><p>Since the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Autonomy_of_1979" class="mw-redirect" title="Statute of Autonomy of 1979">Statute of Autonomy of 1979</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aranese" class="mw-redirect" title="Aranese">Aranese</a> (a dialect of <a href="/wiki/Gascon_dialect" class="mw-redirect" title="Gascon dialect">Gascon</a> <a href="/wiki/Occitan" class="mw-redirect" title="Occitan">Occitan</a>) has also been official and subject to special protection in Val d'Aran. This small area of 7,000 inhabitants was the only place where a dialect of Occitan has received full official status. Then, on 9 August 2006, when the new Statute came into force, Occitan became official throughout Catalonia. Occitan is the mother tongue of 22.4% of the population of Val d'Aran.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Catalan_Sign_Language" title="Catalan Sign Language">Catalan Sign Language</a> is also officially recognised.<sup id="cite_ref-estatut_langs_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-estatut_langs-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although not considered an "official language" in the same way as Catalan, Spanish, and Aranese, <a href="/wiki/Catalan_Sign_Language" title="Catalan Sign Language">Catalan Sign Language</a>, with about 18,000 users in Catalonia,<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> is granted official recognition and support: "The public authorities shall guarantee the use of Catalan sign language and conditions of equality for deaf people who choose to use this language, which shall be the subject of education, protection and respect."<sup id="cite_ref-estatut_langs_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-estatut_langs-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<table cellpadding="3" cellspacing="0" rules="all" style="width:400px; float:right; margin:1em; background:#fff; border:2px solid #aaa; font-size:100%;">
